## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
SE0([Start]) --> SE1{current_event exists?}
SE1 -- No --> SER1([return False])
SE1 -- Yes --> SE2([Compute event_is_post_delivery])
SE2 --> SE3{event.event_type == reopen_event_type?}
SE3 -- No --> SER1
SE3 -- Yes --> SE4{is_ultimate_destination == False?}
SE4 -- No --> SER1
SE4 -- Yes --> SE5{container.lifecycle_state == DELIVERED_STATE.value?}
SE5 -- No --> SER1
SE5 -- Yes --> SE6{event.event_code NOT in ignore_event_codes?}
SE6 -- No --> SER1
SE6 -- Yes --> SE7{NOT (event_code == DEPARTED AND event.location_code == container.origin_location_code)?}
SE7 -- No --> SER1
SE7 -- Yes --> SE8{event_is_post_delivery == True?}
SE8 -- No --> SER1
SE8 -- Yes --> SER2([return True])
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
EX0([Start]) --> EX1{package_delivered_event and package_delivered_event.event_code exists?}
EX1 -- No --> EX2([invoke_ro_event = False])
EX2 --> EXR1([return False])
EX1 -- Yes --> EX3{package_delivered_event.event_code == DELIVERED AND event_type == MILESTONE?}
EX3 -- Yes --> EX4{latest_exception_time > delivered_event_time?}
EX4 -- Yes --> EX5([invoke_ro_event = True])
EX4 -- No --> EX6([invoke_ro_event = False])
EX3 -- No --> EX5
EX5 --> EX7([set reopen_reason = LifecycleStateChangeReasons.DELAYING_EXCEPTIONS_REASON.value])
EX7 --> EXR2([return True])
EX6 --> EXR1
```
